Task instruction sent to agent 
# [TensorRT-LLM] Add W4A8_MXFP4_INT8 Quantization Mode

**Repository:** NVIDIA/TensorRT-LLM  
**Difficulty:** HARD  
**Category:** big_code_feature
**Task Type:** Feature Implementation - Large Codebase

**Reference:** [Trevor's Big Code Research](../../../docs/TREVOR_RESEARCH_DEC2025.md#4-tensorrt-llm-w4a8_mxfp4_int8-quantization-mode)

## Description

Add support for a new quantization mode `W4A8_MXFP4_INT8`—4-bit MXFP4 weights with INT8 activations, targeting Blackwell GPUs. The CUDA kernels already exist on the C++ side; we just need to expose and plumb this through the Python/C++ stack.

Follow the patterns used by the existing `W4A8_MXFP4_FP8` mode—find everywhere that mode is defined, parsed, validated, and used for kernel selection, then add the equivalent support for the INT8 variant. Make sure the Python and C++ quantization enums stay in sync.

Unsupported combinations (certain attention backends, incompatible KV cache settings) should fail at build time with clear errors. Add tests to cover the new mode.

## Task

This task requires implementing code changes to add W4A8_MXFP4_INT8 support.

### Required Implementation

Address implementation concerns in these areas:

1. **Python Quantization Enums**:
   - Find where `W4A8_MXFP4_FP8` is defined in Python code
   - Add `W4A8_MXFP4_INT8` alongside it
   - Update any mode parsing/validation that handles quantization modes

2. **C++ Quantization Enums & Definitions**:
   - Find the C++ enum where quantization modes are defined
   - Add `W4A8_MXFP4_INT8` enum value
   - Ensure Python-C++ enum values stay in sync

3. **Kernel Selection Logic**:
   - Find where the C++ code selects kernels based on quantization mode
   - Add `W4A8_MXFP4_INT8` to the kernel selection logic
   - Route to the appropriate Blackwell GPU kernels

4. **Validation & Constraints**:
   - Find where quantization modes are validated against attention backends
   - Find where KV cache compatibility is checked
   - Add validation rules for unsupported `W4A8_MXFP4_INT8` combinations
   - Ensure build-time errors for incompatible configurations

5. **Python-C++ Bindings**:
   - Update pybind11 or C extension bindings to expose the new mode
   - Ensure Python code can select and use the new mode

6. **Tests & Validation**:
   - Add tests for creating models with `W4A8_MXFP4_INT8` mode
   - Test kernel selection with the new mode
   - Test validation of incompatible combinations
   - Verify build-time errors for unsupported configurations

### Implementation Steps

1. **Understand the quantization architecture**:
   - Find all Python files that reference `W4A8_MXFP4_FP8`
   - Find all C++ files that handle this mode
   - Understand the Python-C++ binding patterns
   - Locate kernel selection and validation logic

2. **Implement Python support**:
   - Add `W4A8_MXFP4_INT8` to Python quantization enums
   - Update parsing/validation to recognize the new mode
   - Update any configuration classes that reference quantization modes

3. **Implement C++ support**:
   - Add `W4A8_MXFP4_INT8` to C++ quantization enum
   - Update kernel selection to handle the new mode
   - Add validation for unsupported combinations (attention backends, KV cache)
   - Generate clear error messages for incompatible configs

4. **Synchronize Python-C++ interface**:
   - Update pybind11 bindings to include new enum value
   - Test round-trip: Python → C++ → kernel selection

5. **Add tests**:
   - Test model creation with new mode
   - Test kernel selection with new mode
   - Test validation of unsupported combinations
   - Test build-time error messages

6. **Verify no regressions**:
   - All tests pass
   - Existing quantization modes still work
   - Build succeeds

## Success Criteria

[x] `W4A8_MXFP4_INT8` enum value defined in Python and C++  
[x] Python code can select and use the new mode  
[x] C++ kernel selection routes to Blackwell GPU kernels  
[x] Validation prevents unsupported mode combinations  
[x] Clear build-time errors for incompatible configurations  
[x] Python and C++ quantization enums stay in sync  
[x] Tests added for mode creation, kernel selection, and validation  
[x] All tests pass  
[x] No regressions in existing quantization modes  
[x] Code follows TensorRT-LLM conventions

```bash
python -m pytest tests/ -v -k "quantization"
```

class QuantMode(IntFlag):
    # [WARNING] KEEP BELOW DEFINITION IN SYNC WITH cpp/tensorrt_llm/common/quantization.h

    # The weights are quantized to 4 bits.
    INT4_WEIGHTS = auto()
    # The weights are quantized to 8 bits.
    INT8_WEIGHTS = auto()
    # The activations are quantized.
    ACTIVATIONS = auto()
    # The method uses one scaling factor per channel. It's pre-computed (static) from the weights.
    PER_CHANNEL = auto()
    # The method uses one scaling factor per token. It's computed on-the-fly.
    PER_TOKEN = auto()
    # The method uses one scaling factor per group. It's pre-computed (static) from the weights.
    PER_GROUP = auto()
    # The KV cache is quantized in INT8.
    INT8_KV_CACHE = auto()
    # The KV cache is quantized in FP8.
    FP8_KV_CACHE = auto()
    # FP8 QDQ
    FP8_QDQ = auto()
    # FP8 rowwise
    FP8_ROWWISE = auto()
    # FP8 block scales for Deepseek
    FP8_1x128_128x128 = auto()
    # W4A8 qserve
    W4A8_QSERVE = auto()
    # FP4
    NVFP4 = auto()
    NVFP4_KV_CACHE = auto()
    # W4A8 NVFP4
    W4A8_NVFP4_FP8 = auto()
    # W4A8 MXFP4
    W4A8_MXFP4_FP8 = auto()
    W4A8_MXFP4_MXFP8 = auto()
    W4A16_MXFP4 = auto()

    # The smallest power-of-two that is not used by a flag. Do not call auto() after that line.
    COUNT = auto()

    # Bitmask to detect if weights, activations or both are quantized.

Do not call auto() after that line.\n    COUNT = auto()\n\n    # Bitmask to detect if weights, activations or both are quantized.\n    WEIGHTS_AND_ACTIVATIONS = INT4_WEIGHTS | INT8_WEIGHTS | ACTIVATIONS\n    # The mask of all valid flags.\n    VALID_FLAGS = COUNT - 1\n\n    def __deepcopy__(self, memo):\n        return self\n\n    # All the bits set? dtype_activation: torch.dtype = torch.bfloat16,\n        gptoss_style: bool = False,\n    ) -> Tuple[bool, Optional[str]]:\n        \"\"\"\n        Check if CutlassFusedMoE can implement the given quantization algorithm.\n\n        CutlassFusedMoE supports:\n        - Unquantized (FP16/BF16): SM >= 80\n        - FP8 per-tensor (QDQ): SM >= 89\n        - FP8_BLOCK_SCALES: SM == 90 only\n        - NVFP4: SM in {100, 103}\n        - W4A8_AWQ: SM in {89, 90} only\n        - W8A16: SM >= 80\n        - W4A16_MXFP4: SM == 90 only\n        - W4A8_MXFP4_FP8: SM in {100, 103}\n        - W4A8_MXFP4_MXFP8: SM in {100, 103}\n\n        Args:\n            quant_algo: The quantization algorithm to check (None for unquantized)\n            dtype_activation: The activation input data type (before quantization).\n                Supported dtypes vary by quantization mode:\n                - Unquantized: float16, bfloat16\n                - FP8/FP8_BLOCK_SCALES/W4A8_MXFP4_FP8: float16, bfloat16, float32\n                - NVFP4: float16, bfloat16, float8_e4m3fn\n                - W4A16_MXFP4/W4A8_AWQ/W8A16/W4A8_MXFP4_MXFP8: float16, bfloat16\n            gptoss_style: Whether gptoss_style (bias/swiglu with custom alpha/beta/limit) is enabled.\n                CutlassFusedMoE only supports gptoss_style for W4A8_MXFP4_MXFP8 quantization.\n\n        Returns:\n            Tuple[bool, Optional[str]]: (can_implement, skip_reason)\n        \"\"\"\n        from .interface import _warn_and_return\n\n        sm_version = get_sm_version()\n\n        # Check minimum SM version for Cutlass backend\n        if sm_version < 80:\n            return _warn_and_return(\n                f\"CutlassFusedMoE requires SM >= 80, got SM{sm_version}\")\n\n        # Check gptoss_style support\n        if gptoss_style and quant_algo not in cls._GPTOSS_SUPPORTED_ALGOS:\n            return _warn_and_return(\n                f\"CutlassFusedMoE gptoss_style only supports W4A8_MXFP4_MXFP8 \"\n                f\"(got quant_algo={quant_algo})\")\n\n        # Check if quant_algo is supported\n        if quant_algo not in cls._QUANT_SUPPORT_TABLE:\n            return _warn_and_return(\n                f\"CutlassFusedMoE does not support quant_algo={quant_algo}\")\n\n        support_info = cls._QUANT_SUPPORT_TABLE[quant_algo]\n\n        # Check SM version constraint\n        constraint_type, constraint_value = support_info[\"sm_constraint\"]\n        algo_name = \"unquantized\" if quant_algo is None else quant_algo.name\n\n        if constraint_type == \"min\":\n            if sm_version < constraint_value:\n                return _warn_and_return(\n                    f\"CutlassFusedMoE {algo_name} requires SM >= {constraint_value}, \"\n                    f\"got SM{sm_version}\")\n        elif constraint_type == \"exact\":\n            if sm_version != constraint_value:\n                return _warn_and_return(\n                    f\"CutlassFusedMoE {algo_name} only supports SM{constraint_value}, \"\n                    f\"got SM{sm_version}\")\n        elif constraint_type == \"in\":\n            if sm_version not in constraint_value:\n                sm_list = \"/\".join(f\"SM{v}\" for v in sorted(constraint_value))\n                return _warn_and_return(\n                    f\"CutlassFusedMoE {algo_name} only supports {sm_list}, \"\n                    f\"got SM{sm_version}\")\n\n        # Check dtype_activation\n        supported_dtypes = support_info[\"dtypes\"]\n        if dtype_activation not in supported_dtypes:\n            dtype_list = \", \".join(str(d) for d in supported_dtypes)\n            return _warn_and_return(\n                f\"CutlassFusedMoE {algo_name} requires {dtype_list}, \"\n                f\"got {dtype_activation}\")\n\n        return True, None\n\n    def __init__(\n        self,\n        *,\n        routing_method: BaseMoeRoutingMethod,\n        num_experts: int,\n        hidden_size: int,\n        intermediate_size: int,\n        dtype: Optional[torch.dtype] = None,\n        reduce_results: bool = False,\n        model_config: ModelConfig = ModelConfig(),\n        aux_stream_dict: Optional[Dict[AuxStreamType,\n                                       torch.cuda.Stream]] = None,\n        weight_loading_mode: MoEWeightLoadingMode = MoEWeightLoadingMode.\n        VANILLA,\n        bias: bool = False,\n        apply_router_weight_on_input: bool = False,\n        layer_idx: Optional[int] = None,\n        swiglu_alpha: Optional[torch.Tensor] = None,\n        swiglu_beta: Optional[torch.Tensor] = None,\n        swiglu_limit: Optional[torch.Tensor] = None,\n        init_load_balancer: bool = True,\n        without_comm: bool = False,\n        activation_type: ActivationType = ActivationType.Swiglu,\n    ):\n\n        super().__init__(\n            routing_method=routing_method,\n            num_experts=num_experts,\n            hidden_size=hidden_size,\n            intermediate_size=intermediate_size,\n            dtype=dtype,\n            reduce_results=reduce_results,\n            model_config=model_config,\n            weight_loading_mode=weight_loading_mode,\n            bias=bias,\n            swiglu_alpha=swiglu_alpha,\n            swiglu_beta=swiglu_beta,\n            swiglu_limit=swiglu_limit,\n            layer_idx=layer_idx,\n            init_load_balancer=init_load_balancer,\n            activation_type=activation_type,\n        )\n\n        # Store original hidden size before any potential padding\n        self.unpadded_hidden_size = self.hidden_size\n\n        if model_config.quant_config and model_config.quant_config.layer_quant_mode.has_w4a16_mxfp4(\n        ):\n            self.hidden_size = ((self.hidden_size + 127) // 128) * 128\n            self.intermediate_size_per_partition = (\n                (self.intermediate_size_per_partition + 127) // 128) * 128\n\n        # Note: num_slots, expert_size_per_partition, initial_global_assignments,\n        # slot_start, slot_end, initial_local_expert_ids are all initialized by\n        # base class's _init_load_balancer() method\n\n        # moe_max_num_tokens is set in ModelConfig.__post_init__ if not specified\n        # The default value is max_num_tokens * dp_size\n        self.moe_max_num_tokens = model_config.moe_max_num_tokens\n        # The auxiliary CUDA stream and CUDA events are only used when MoE chunking is applied\n        default_moe_max_num_tokens = model_config.max_num_tokens * model_config.mapping.dp_size\n        if self.moe_max_num_tokens < default_moe_max_num_tokens:\n            self.aux_stream = aux_stream_dict[\n                AuxStreamType.\n                MoeChunkingOverlap] if aux_stream_dict is not None else torch.cuda.Stream(\n                )\n            self.event_dict = {\n                key: torch.cuda.Event()\n                for key in [EventType.Main, EventType.MoeChunkingOverlap]\n            }\n        else:\n            self.aux_stream = None\n            self.event_dict = None\n\n        # The profiler converges on the same best tactic when the number of tokens is large enough.\n        # To avoid long profiling time, the max number of tokens used in the profiling is capped to\n        # around 16k tokens per expert, which is well into the compute bound domain.\n        self.tune_max_num_tokens = min(\n            self.moe_max_num_tokens,\n            16384 * self.num_slots // routing_method.get_experts_per_token(),\n        )\n        self.has_been_profiled = False\n        self.has_been_profiled_min_latency = False\n\n        # When without_comm=True, skip communication initialization (ConfigurableMoE will handle it)\n        if not without_comm:\n            self.alltoall_method_type = self.select_alltoall_method_type()\n            logger.info_once(\n                f\"{self.__class__.__name__} selects alltoall_method_type {self.alltoall_method_type!r}\",\n                key=\"alltoall_method_type\")\n            self.alltoall_workspace = None\n            self.alltoall_prepare_workspace = None\n            self.use_low_precision_combine = False\n            if self.enable_alltoall:\n                self.use_low_precision_combine = model_config.use_low_precision_moe_combine\n\n                if self.alltoall_method_type == AlltoallMethodType.NVLinkTwoSided:\n                    MnnvlMemory.initialize()\n                    self.alltoall_workspace = MnnvlMoe.get_moe_workspaces(\n                        model_config.mapping)\n                    self.alltoall_prepare_workspace = MnnvlMoe.get_moe_prepare_workspace(\n                        model_config.mapping)\n                elif self.alltoall_method_type == AlltoallMethodType.NVLinkOneSided:\n                    # Calculate required workspace size\n                    ep_size = self.mapping.moe_ep_size\n                    max_num_tokens = model_config.max_num_tokens\n                    hidden_size = self.hidden_size\n                    dtype = self.dtype or torch.float16\n\n                    workspace_size = MoeAlltoAll.calculate_required_workspace_size(\n                        ep_size,\n                        self.routing_method.experts_per_token,\n                        max_num_tokens,\n                        hidden_size,\n                        dtype,\n                        self.num_experts if self.layer_load_balancer else None,\n                    )\n\n                    self.moe_a2a = MoeAlltoAll(\n                        mapping=self.mapping,\n                        max_num_tokens=model_config.max_num_tokens,\n                        top_k=self.routing_method.experts_per_token,\n                        num_slots=self.num_slots,\n                        workspace_size_per_rank=workspace_size,\n                        num_experts=self.num_experts\n                        if self.layer_load_balancer else None,\n                    )\n                elif self.alltoall_method_type == AlltoallMethodType.DeepEP or self.alltoall_method_type == AlltoallMethodType.DeepEPLowLatency:\n                    raise NotImplementedError(\n                        \"DeepEP and DeepEPLowLatency are not supported for CutlassFusedMoE yet\"\n                    )\n                else:\n                    raise NotImplementedError(\n                        f\"Unsupported alltoall method type: {self.alltoall_method_type!r}\"\n                    )\n        else:\n            # When without_comm=True, set minimal attributes\n            # Communication will be handled by parent wrapper (e.g., ConfigurableMoE)\n            self.alltoall_method_type = AlltoallMethodType.NotEnabled\n            self.alltoall_workspace = None\n            self.alltoall_prepare_workspace = None\n            self.use_low_precision_combine = False\n            self.moe_a2a = None\n\n        # If True, the router weight will be multiplied on the input rather than at the end of FC2\n        self.apply_router_weight_on_input = apply_router_weight_on_input\n\n        # Finalize fusion should be disabled if Lora is used.\n        self.use_fused_finalize = not model_config.moe_disable_finalize_fusion and model_config.lora_config is None\n\n        self._weights_created = False\n        if not model_config.skip_create_weights_in_init:\n            self.create_weights()\n\n    def _check_configs(self):\n        assert self._weights_created\n\n        if self.apply_router_weight_on_input:\n            assert self.routing_method.top_k == 1, \"Current walkaround only supports top-1 routing\"\n\n        if self.quant_config and self.quant_config.quant_mode.has_any_quant(\n                exclude_kv_cache=True):\n            if not (self.quant_config.quant_mode.has_nvfp4()\n                    | self.quant_config.quant_mode.has_fp8_block_scales()\n                    | self.quant_config.quant_mode.has_fp8_qdq()\n                    | self.quant_config.quant_mode.is_weight_only()\n                    | self.quant_config.quant_mode.has_w4a8_mxfp4_fp8()\n                    | self.quant_config.quant_mode.has_w4a16_mxfp4()\n                    | self.quant_config.quant_mode.has_w4a8_mxfp4_mxfp8()):\n                raise ValueError(\n                    f\"unsupported quantization mode: {self.quant_config.quant_mode}\"\n                )\n\n    @property\n    def has_w4afp8(self):\n        assert self._weights_created\n        return self.quant_config and self.quant_config.quant_mode.is_int4_weight_only_per_group(\n        )\n\n    @property\n    def has_int8_woq_per_channel(self):\n        return self.quant_config and self.quant_config.layer_quant_mode.is_int8_weight_only(\n        ) and not self.quant_config.layer_quant_mode.has_per_group_scaling()\n\n    def select_alltoall_method_type(self) -> AlltoallMethodType:\n        # If no attention DP, no need to use AlltoAll.\n        if self.mapping.dp_size == 1:\n            return AlltoallMethodType.NotEnabled\n\n        # AlltoAll cannot support MoE TP.\n        if self.mapping.moe_tp_size != 1:\n            return AlltoallMethodType.NotEnabled\n\n        if not MnnvlMemory.supports_mnnvl():\n            return AlltoallMethodType.NotEnabled\n\n        all2all_method_type = os.environ.get(\"TRTLLM_FORCE_ALLTOALL_METHOD\")\n        if all2all_method_type is not None:\n            if AlltoallMethodType[all2all_method_type] in [\n                    AlltoallMethodType.DeepEP,\n                    AlltoallMethodType.DeepEPLowLatency\n            ]:\n                raise NotImplementedError(\n                    \"DeepEP and DeepEPLowLatency are not supported for CutlassFusedMoE yet\"\n                )\n            return AlltoallMethodType[all2all_method_type]\n\n        # TODO: We found that NVLinkOneSided performs better than NCCL AllGather/ReduceScatter,\n        # regardless of the relationship between EP size and topK. We favor NVLinkOneSided for now.\n        # if not self.mapping.moe_ep_size > self.routing_method.experts_per_token:\n        #     return AlltoallMethodType.NotEnabled\n        return AlltoallMethodType.NVLinkOneSided\n\n    @cached_property\n    def enable_alltoall(self):\n        \"\"\" enable_alltoall (bool): whether to enable alltoall instead of allgather/reducescatter\n        \"\"\"\n        return self.alltoall_method_type != AlltoallMethodType.NotEnabled\n\n    def quantize_input(\n        self,\n        x: Union[torch.Tensor, Fp4QuantizedTensor],\n        post_quant_comm: bool = True,\n        **kwargs,\n    ) -> Tuple[torch.Tensor, Optional[torch.Tensor]]:\n        \"\"\"\n        Quantize input tensor - CutlassFusedMoE implementation\n\n        Handles all quantization cases for Cutlass backend.\n\n        Args:\n            x: Input tensor to quantize\n            post_quant_comm: Whether this is for post-quantization communication\n                           (allgather or alltoall). If True, x_sf will be reshaped to 2D.\n\n        Returns:\n            Tuple of (quantized_x, x_sf)\n        \"\"\"\n        x_sf = None\n        if self.has_any_quant:\n            if self.has_fp8_qdq or self.has_w4a8_mxfp4_fp8:\n                x, _ = torch.ops.tensorrt_llm.static_quantize_e4m3_per_tensor(\n                    x, self.fc31_input_dequant)\n            elif self.has_deepseek_fp8_block_scales:\n                # No quantization needed here, handled in kernel\n                pass\n            elif self.has_w4afp8:\n                # No quantization needed here, handled in kernel\n                pass\n            elif self.has_w4a16_mxfp4:\n                pad_size = self.hidden_size - x.shape[1]\n                x = torch.nn.functional.pad(x, (0, pad_size))\n            elif self.has_int8_woq_per_channel:\n                # No quantization needed here, handled in kernel\n                pass\n            elif self.has_nvfp4:\n                if hasattr(\n                        self,\n                        'fc31_act_scale') and self.fc31_act_scale is not None:\n                    assert not isinstance(\n                        x, Fp4QuantizedTensor\n                    ), \"Fp4QuantizedTensor is not expected for AWQ quantization.\"\n                    x = x * self.fc31_act_scale\n                # Quantize based on communication scenario\n                if post_quant_comm:\n                    if isinstance(x, Fp4QuantizedTensor):\n                        assert not x.is_sf_swizzled, \"Fp4QuantizedTensor should not be swizzled before communication\"\n                        x, x_sf = x.fp4_tensor, x.scaling_factor\n                        x_row = x.shape[0]\n                    else:\n                        x_row = x.shape[0]\n                        x, x_sf = torch.ops.trtllm.fp4_quantize(\n                            x, self.fc31_input_scale, self.scaling_vector_size,\n                            False, False)\n                    # Reshape x_sf to 2D for post-quant communication\n                    if x_sf is not None:\n                        x_sf = x_sf.view((x_row, -1))\n                else:\n                    if not isinstance(x, Fp4QuantizedTensor):\n                        x, x_sf = torch.ops.trtllm.fp4_quantize(\n                            x, self.fc31_input_scale, self.scaling_vector_size,\n                            False, True)\n            elif self.has_w4a8_mxfp4_mxfp8:\n                if post_quant_comm:\n                    x, x_sf = torch.ops.trtllm.mxfp8_quantize(\n                        x, False, alignment=self.quant_method.weight_alignment)\n                    # Reshape x_sf to 2D for post-quant communication\n                    # x.shape[0] is padded\n                    if x_sf is not None:\n                        x_sf = x_sf.view((x.shape[0], -1))\n                else:\n                    x, x_sf = torch.ops.trtllm.mxfp8_quantize(\n                        x, True, alignment=self.quant_method.weight_alignment)\n            else:\n                raise ValueError(\n                    f\"unsupported quantization mode: {self.quant_config.quant_mode}\"\n                )\n\n        return x, x_sf\n\n    def _supports_load_balancer(self) -> bool:\n        \"\"\"CutlassFusedMoE supports load balancer.\"\"\"\n        return True\n\n    def _get_quant_method(self):\n        if self.quant_config is not None and self.quant_config.layer_quant_mode.has_any_quant(\n                exclude_kv_cache=True):\n            if self.quant_config.layer_quant_mode.has_fp8_qdq():\n                return FP8QDQFusedMoEMethod()\n            elif self.quant_config.layer_quant_mode.has_fp8_block_scales():\n                return DeepSeekFP8BlockScalesFusedMoEMethod()\n            elif self.quant_config.layer_quant_mode.has_nvfp4():\n                return NVFP4CutlassFusedMoEMethod()\n            elif self.quant_config.layer_quant_mode.is_int4_weight_only_per_group(\n            ):\n                return WInt4AFP8FusedMoEMethod()\n            elif self.has_int8_woq_per_channel:\n                return INT8WoqPerChannelFusedMoEMethod()\n            elif self.quant_config.layer_quant_mode.has_w4a8_mxfp4_fp8():\n                return W4A8MXFP4FP8CutlassFusedMoEMethod()\n            elif self.quant_config.layer_quant_mode.has_w4a16_mxfp4():\n                return WFP4A16FusedMoEMethod()\n            elif self.quant_config.layer_quant_mode.has_w4a8_mxfp4_mxfp8():\n                return W4A8MXFP4MXFP8CutlassFusedMoEMethod()\n            else:\n                raise ValueError(\n                    f\"Unsupported quantization mode: {self.quant_config.quant_mode}\"\n                )\n        else:\n            return UnquantizedFusedMoEMethod()\n\n    def create_weights(self):\n        if self._weights_created:\n            return\n\n        self.quant_method = self._get_quant_method()\n        self.quant_method.create_weights(self)\n\n        self._weights_created = True\n        self._check_configs()\n\n    def supports_moe_output_in_alltoall_workspace(self):\n        return True\n\n    def run_moe(\n        self,\n        x: torch.Tensor,\n        token_selected_experts: torch.Tensor,\n        token_final_scales: torch.Tensor,\n        x_sf: Optional[torch.Tensor] = None,\n        is_sf_swizzled: bool = True,\n        output_dtype: Optional[torch.dtype] = None,\n        tuner_num_tokens: Optional[int] = None,\n        tuner_top_k: Optional[int] = None,\n        moe_output: Optional[torch.Tensor] = None,\n        enable_alltoall: Optional[bool] = None,\n    ) -> torch.Tensor:\n        \"\"\"\n        Run MoE computation with Cutlass backend.\n\n        This method encapsulates the core MoE computation logic, handling different\n        quantization schemes.\n\n        Args:\n            x: Input hidden states (may be pre-quantized)\n            token_selected_experts: Expert IDs or expert slots [num_tokens, top_k]\n                                   If EPLB is enabled, represents expert slots; otherwise expert IDs\n            token_final_scales: Final scaling factors for each token\n            x_sf: Input scale factors (optional, for certain quantization schemes)\n            is_sf_swizzled: Whether scaling factors are swizzled\n            output_dtype: Output data type (optional)\n            tuner_num_tokens: Number of tokens for profiling tuner (optional)\n            tuner_top_k: Top-k value for profiling tuner (optional)\n            moe_output: Pre-allocated output buffer (optional)\n            enable_alltoall: Whether alltoall communication is enabled (optional). If None, defaults to self.enable_alltoall.\n\n        Returns:\n            final_hidden_states: Output tensor from MoE computation\n        \"\"\"\n        # Determine weight dtype based on quantization mode\n        weight_dtype = self.w3_w1_weight.dtype\n        if self.has_any_quant:\n            if self.has_w4afp8:\n                weight_dtype = torch.quint4x2\n            elif self.has_w4a16_mxfp4:\n                weight_dtype = torch.uint8\n\n        if enable_alltoall is None:\n            enable_alltoall = self.enable_alltoall\n\n        result = torch.ops.trtllm.fused_moe(\n            x,\n            token_selected_experts,\n            token_final_scales,\n            self.w3_w1_weight.view(weight_dtype),\n            self.w3_w1_bias,\n            self.w2_weight.view(weight_dtype),\n            self.w2_bias,\n            output_dtype,\n            quant_scales=self.quant_scales,\n            input_sf=x_sf,\n            swizzled_input_sf=is_sf_swizzled,\n            swiglu_alpha=self.swiglu_alpha,\n            swiglu_beta=self.swiglu_beta,\n            swiglu_limit=self.swiglu_limit,\n            tp_size=self.tp_size,\n            tp_rank=self.tp_rank,\n            ep_size=self.ep_size,\n            ep_rank=self.ep_rank,\n            cluster_size=self.cluster_size,\n            cluster_rank=self.cluster_rank,\n            enable_alltoall=enable_alltoall,\n            use_deepseek_fp8_block_scale=self.has_deepseek_fp8_block_scales,\n            use_w4_group_scaling=self.has_w4afp8 or self.has_w4a16_mxfp4,\n            use_int8_woq_per_channel=self.has_int8_woq_per_channel,\n            use_mxfp8_act_scaling=self.has_w4a8_mxfp4_mxfp8,\n            min_latency_mode=False,\n            use_fused_finalize=self.use_fused_finalize,\n            tune_max_num_tokens=self.tune_max_num_tokens,\n            tuner_num_tokens=tuner_num_tokens,\n            tuner_top_k=tuner_top_k,\n            activation_type=self.activation_type,\n            unpadded_hidden_size=self.unpadded_hidden_size,\n            out_tensor=moe_output,\n        )\n        # When moe_output is provided, the result is written in-place and\n        # fused_moe returns empty list to avoid aliasing constraint violation.\n        # Otherwise, unpack the single tensor from the returned list.\n        if moe_output is not None:\n            final_hidden_states = moe_output\n        else:\n            final_hidden_states = result[0]\n\n        return final_hidden_states\n\n    def forward_chunk(\n            self,\n            x: Union[torch.Tensor, Fp4QuantizedTensor],\n            router_logits: torch.Tensor,\n            output_dtype: Optional[torch.dtype] = None,\n            all_rank_num_tokens: Optional[List[int]] = None,\n            use_dp_padding: Optional[bool] = None,\n            repeating_info: tuple = (True, True),\n    ) -> torch.Tensor:\n        if isinstance(x, Fp4QuantizedTensor):\n            assert output_dtype is not None\n        else:\n            output_dtype = x.dtype\n\n        is_first_call, is_last_call = repeating_info\n\n        self._load_balancer_start_wait_gpu_stage(is_first_call)\n\n        # apply routing\n        token_selected_experts, token_final_scales = self.routing_method.apply(\n            router_logits)\n        assert token_selected_experts.shape[\n            1] == self.routing_method.experts_per_token\n        assert token_selected_experts.shape == token_final_scales.shape\n        assert token_selected_experts.shape[0] == router_logits.shape[0]\n        assert token_final_scales.dtype == torch.float32\n        assert token_selected_experts.dtype == torch.int32\n\n        if self.layer_load_balancer:\n            self._load_balancer_done_wait_gpu_stage(is_first_call)\n            ignore_allreduce = self.enable_alltoall and self.alltoall_method_type in (\n                AlltoallMethodType.NVLinkTwoSided,\n                AlltoallMethodType.NVLinkOneSided,\n            )\n            self._load_balancer_update_statistic(\n                token_selected_experts,\n                is_first_call,\n                is_last_call,\n                ignore_allreduce=ignore_allreduce)\n            token_selected_slots = self._load_balancer_route(\n                token_selected_experts, self.use_dp)\n        else:\n            token_selected_slots = token_selected_experts\n\n        # If load balancer is disabled, the statistics are collected from expert IDs.\n        # If load balancer is enabled, the statistics are collected from expert slot IDs.\n        ExpertStatistic.set_layer(self.layer_idx)\n        ExpertStatistic.maybe_add_info(self.num_slots, token_selected_slots)\n        token_selected_slots = get_calibrator().maybe_collect_or_replay_slots(\n            self.num_slots, not 1\ndef swiglu_torch(a: torch.Tensor, alpha: float, beta: float,\n                 limit: Optional[float]) -> torch.Tensor:\n    a_glu = a[..., ::2]\n    if limit is not None:\n        a_glu = a_glu.clamp(max=limit)\n    a_linear = a[..., 1::2]\n    if limit is not None:\n        a_linear = a_linear.clamp(min=-limit, max=limit)\n\n    out_glu = a_glu * torch.sigmoid(alpha * a_glu)\n    out = out_glu * (a_linear + beta)\n    return out\n\n\ndef shuffle_weight_for_activation_kernel(\n        w3_w1_weight: torch.Tensor) -> torch.Tensor:\n    temp_weight = w3_w1_weight.clone()\n    last_dim = w3_w1_weight.shape[-1]\n    assert w3_w1_weight.dim() in [1, 2, 3]\n    # n_dims = 1: Single expert bias (like the unquantized case)\n    # n_dims = 2: Single expert weight (like the unquantized case)\n    # n_dims = 3: Multiple experts weight (re-quantization for fp8 qdq)\n    w3_w1_weight[..., 0::2] = temp_weight[..., last_dim // 2:]\n    w3_w1_weight[..., 1::2] = temp_weight[..., 0:last_dim // 2]\n    return w3_w1_weight\n\n\n# This kernel remaps the global routing information (bitmatrix and indices)\n# to a local view for this specific EP worker.\n#\n# The bitmask is shifted so that the worker's slice of experts starts at bit 0.\n# Since the slice may not align with 32-bit word boundaries, this is done by\n# loading two consecutive words (v1, v2) and \"stitching\" the result together.\n# The expression `(v1 >> start_bit) | (v2 << (32 - start_bit))` takes the\n# upper bits from v1 and combines them with the lower bits from v2 to form the\n# new, correctly aligned word.\n@triton.jit\ndef _routing_shift_bitmatrix_range(Bitmatrix, stride_bm, stride_bn, Indices,\n                                   stride_im, stride_in, n_words, n_cols,\n                                   slice_start, slice_end,\n                                   BLOCK_N: tl.constexpr):\n    pid_m = tl.program_id(0)\n    start_word = slice_start // 32\n    start_bit = slice_start % 32\n\n    for col0 in range(0, n_words, BLOCK_N):\n        w = col0 + tl.arange(0, BLOCK_N)  # dst\u2010word indices\n        dst_mask = w < n_words\n\n        # corresponding source words (and the next word for carry bits)\n        src1_w = start_word + w\n        src2_w = src1_w + 1\n\n        ptr1 = Bitmatrix + pid_m * stride_bm + src1_w * stride_bn\n        ptr2 = Bitmatrix + pid_m * stride_bm + src2_w * stride_bn\n\n        v1 = tl.load(ptr1, mask=src1_w < n_words, other=0).to(tl.uint32)\n        v2 = tl.load(ptr2, mask=src2_w < n_words, other=0).to(tl.uint32)\n\n        # shift the slice down to bit\u20100\n        shifted = tl.where(start_bit == 0, v1,\n                           (v1 >> start_bit) | (v2 << (32 - start_bit)))\n\n        # write back in place; bits past the region are already zero\n        tl.store(Bitmatrix + pid_m * stride_bm + w * stride_bn,\n                 shifted.to(tl.int32),\n                 mask=dst_mask)\n\n    # Fix the indices associated with the bitmatrix.\n    for col0 in range(0, n_cols, BLOCK_N):\n        offs = col0 + tl.arange(0, BLOCK_N)\n        mask_i = offs < n_cols\n\n        ptr = Indices + pid_m * stride_im + offs * stride_in\n        yi = tl.load(ptr, mask=mask_i, other=0).to(tl.int32)\n\n        yi = tl.where(yi < slice_end, yi - slice_start,\n                      yi)  # shift inside slice\n        yi = tl.where(yi < 0, yi + slice_end, yi)  # wrap negatives\n\n        tl.store(ptr, yi, mask=mask_i)\n\n\nclass TritonEPRouter():\n\n    def prune_routing_ep(self, expt_scal, expt_indx, bitmatrix, n_expts_tot,\n                         slice_start, slice_end):\n        from triton_kernels.compaction import compaction\n        from triton_kernels.routing import _routing_clear_bitmatrix\n        n_tokens_pad = expt_scal.shape[0]\n        _routing_shift_bitmatrix_range[(n_tokens_pad, )](\n            bitmatrix.storage.data,\n            bitmatrix.storage.data.stride(0),\n expt_indx.shape[1],\n            slice_start,\n            slice_end,\n            BLOCK_N=512,\n        )\n        _routing_clear_bitmatrix[(n_tokens_pad, )](\n            bitmatrix.storage.data,\n            bitmatrix.storage.data.stride(0),\n            bitmatrix.storage.data.stride(1),\n            bitmatrix.storage.data.shape[1],\n            slice_end - slice_start,\n            BLOCK_N=512,\n        )\n        # perform compaction to update expt_scal / expt_indx\n        expt_scal, expt_indx = compaction(expt_scal, expt_indx, bitmatrix)\n        n_expts_tot = slice_end - slice_start\n        bitmatrix.shape[-1] = n_expts_tot\n        return expt_scal, expt_indx, bitmatrix\n\n    def __call__(self,\n                 logits,\n                 n_expts_act,\n                 sm_first=False,\n                 expt_indx=None,\n                 ep=1,\n                 node_idx=0,\n                 n_rows=None):\n        n_expts_tot = logits.shape[-1]\n        n_expts_local = n_expts_tot // ep\n        slice_start = node_idx * n_expts_local\n        slice_end = slice_start + n_expts_local\n\n        from triton_kernels.routing import routing_from_bitmatrix\n        from triton_kernels.topk import topk\n        if sm_first:\n            logits = torch.softmax(logits, dim=-1)\n        expt_scal, expt_indx, bitmatrix = topk(logits,\n                                               n_expts_act,\n                                               apply_softmax=not sm_first,\n                expt_scal, expt_indx, bitmatrix, n_expts_tot, slice_start,\n                slice_end)\n        return routing_from_bitmatrix(bitmatrix, expt_scal, expt_indx,\n                                      n_expts_local, n_expts_act)\n\n\ndef maybe_update_stride(weight):\n    assert weight.dim() == 3\n    # For the latest Triton kernels, w.stride(-2)==1 works universally\n    return    f\"TRITON_MOE_MXFP4_NUM_WARPS should be 4 or 8, got {num_warps}\"\n    value_layout, value_layout_opts = layout.make_default_matmul_mxfp4_w_layout(\n        mx_axis=1)\n    scale_layout, H20\":\n        from triton_kernels.tensor_details.layout_details.strided import \\\n            StridedLayout\n        value_layout = StridedLayout\n        value_layout_opts = dict()\n        scale_layout = StridedLayout\n        scale_layout_opts = dict()\n\n    opt = {\"value_layout\": value_layout, \"value_layout_opts\": value_layout_opts, \\\n            \"scale_layout\": scale_layout, \"scale_layout_opts\": scale_layout_opts}\n\n    # w, w_scale = downcast_to_mxfp(tensor.to(torch.bfloat16), torch.uint8, axis=1)\n    w = convert_layout(wrap_torch_tensor(w, dtype=FP4), opt[\"value_layout\"],\n                       **opt[\"value_layout_opts\"])\n    w_scale = convert_layout(wrap_torch_tensor(w_scale), opt[\"scale_layout\"],\n                             **opt[\"scale_layout_opts\"])\n    return w, w_scale\n\n\ndef get_padded_size(size: int, padding: int) -> int:\n    return ((size + padding - 1) // padding) * padding\n\n\n# Pad both n and k dimensions, then shard along shard_axis\n# Handles weights, scales, and biases, which are expected to be 1D or 2D tensors.\ndef shard_and_pad_tensor(\n    tensor: torch.Tensor,\n    shard_axis: int,\n    n_alignment: int,\n    k_alignment: int,\n    tp_size: int,\n    tp_rank: int,\n    device: torch.device,\n) -> torch.Tensor:\n    assert tensor.dim() in (1,\n                            2), \"Expecting single expect gemm weights or biases\"\n    assert shard_axis in (0, 1), \"Shard axis must be 0 or 1\"\n\n    padding = [n_alignment, k_alignment]\n    size_to_pad = [0] * 2\n\n    tensor = tensor.to(device)\n\n    # First we pad the sharded axis\n    if shard_axis < tensor.dim():\n        padded_size = get_padded_size(tensor.shape[shard_axis],\n                                      padding[shard_axis] * tp_size)\n        assert 0 <= tp_rank < tp_size\n        assert tensor.shape[shard_axis] <= padded_size\n        assert padded_size % tp_size == 0\n\n        shard_size = padded_size // tp_size\n        shard_start = tp_rank * shard_size\n        assert shard_start < tensor.shape[shard_axis]\n        shard_end = min(shard_start + shard_size, tensor.shape[shard_axis])\n        actual_size = shard_end - shard_start\n\n        tensor = tensor.narrow(shard_axis, shard_start, actual_size)\n        size_to_pad[shard_axis] = shard_size - actual_size\n\n    # Now we pad the non-sharded axis\n    non_shard_axis = 1 - shard_axis\n    if non_shard_axis < tensor.dim():\n        padded_size = get_padded_size(tensor.shape[non_shard_axis],\n                                      padding[non_shard_axis])\n        size_to_pad[non_shard_axis] = padded_size - tensor.shape[non_shard_axis]\n\n    # Actually call pad\n    if any(size_to_pad):\n        pad = (0, size_to_pad[0]) if tensor.dim() == 1 else (0, size_to_pad[1],\n                                                             0, size_to_pad[0])\n        tensor = torch.nn.functional.pad(tensor, pad)\n\n    return tensor\n\n\n# We inherit from TritonUnquantizedFusedMoEMethod to reuse the weight preprocessing logic\nclass TritonMXFP4FusedMoEMethod(TritonUnquantizedFusedMoEMethod):\n\n    def __init__(self, activation_dtype):\n        super().__init__(shuffle_weight=True)\n        assert activation_dtype in [torch.float8_e4m3fn, torch.bfloat16], \\\n            f\"TritonMXFP4FusedMoEMethod only supports float8_e4m3fn or bfloat16 activation, got {activation_dtype}\"\n        self.activation_dtype = activation_dtype\n\n        self.k_alignment = 128\n        self.n_alignment = 2 * self.k_alignment\n\n    def create_weights(self, module: torch.nn.Module):\n        weight_dtype = torch.uint8\n\n        # The Triton kernel accepts the w3_w1_weight in (num_experts, hidden_dim, intermediate_dim * 2) format\n        w3_w1_weight_shape = (\n            module.expert_size_per_partition,\n            get_padded_size(module.hidden_size, self.k_alignment) //\n            2,  # Two mxfp4 packed to a byte\n            get_padded_size(module.intermediate_size_per_partition * 2,\n                            self.n_alignment),\n        )\n\n        w3_w1_scale_shape = (\n            w3_w1_weight_shape[0],\n            w3_w1_weight_shape[1] //\n            16,  # block size of 32 for mxfp4, we already divided by 2 before so only divide by 16\n            w3_w1_weight_shape[2],\n        )\n\n        # The Triton kernel accepts the w2_weight in (num_experts, intermediate_dim, hidden_dim) format\n        w2_weight_shape = (\n            module.expert_size_per_partition,\n            get_padded_size(module.intermediate_size_per_partition,\n                            self.k_alignment) //\n            2,  # Two mxfp4 packed to a byte,\n            get_padded_size(module.hidden_size, self.n_alignment),\n        )\n\n        w2_scale_shape = (\n            w2_weight_shape[0],\n            w2_weight_shape[1] //\n            16,  # block size of 32 for mxfp4, we already divided by 2 before so only divide by 16\n            w2_weight_shape[2],\n        )\n\n        w3_w1_bias_shape = (w3_w1_weight_shape[0], w3_w1_weight_shape[2])\n        w2_bias_shape = (w2_weight_shape[0], w2_weight_shape[2])\n\n        FusedMoEMethodBase.create_weights(self,\n                                          module,\n                                          weight_dtype,\n                                          w3_w1_weight_shape,\n                                          w2_weight_shape,\n                                          bias_dtype=torch.float32,\n                                          w3_w1_bias_shape=w3_w1_bias_shape,\n                                          w2_bias_shape=w2_bias_shape)\n\n        fc31_dequant = nn.Parameter(\n            torch.empty(w3_w1_scale_shape, dtype=torch.uint8),  # mxfp8 scale\n            requires_grad=False)\n        module.register_parameter(\"fc31_dequant\", fc31_dequant)\n\n        fc2_dequant = nn.Parameter(\n            torch.empty(w2_scale_shape, dtype=torch.uint8),  # mxfp8 scale\n            requires_grad=False)\n        module.register_parameter(\"fc2_dequant\", fc2_dequant)\n\n        if self.activation_dtype == torch.float8_e4m3fn:\n            fc31_input_dequant = nn.Parameter(torch.tensor(1.,\n                                                           dtype=torch.float32),\n                                              requires_grad=False)\n            module.register_parameter(\"fc31_input_dequant\", fc31_input_dequant)\n\n            fc2_input_dequant = nn.Parameter(torch.tensor(1.,\n                                                          dtype=torch.float32),\n                                             requires_grad=False)\n            module.register_parameter(\"fc2_input_dequant\", fc2_input_dequant)\n\n        self.setup_quant_scales(module)\n\n    def setup_quant_scales(self, module: torch.nn.Module):\n        module.quant_scales = TritonMXFP4FusedMoEQuantScales(\n            fc1_dequant=module.fc31_dequant,\n            fc2_dequant=module.fc2_dequant,\n            fc1_input_dequant=getattr(\n                module, 'fc31_input_dequant',\n                None),  # activation scale exists only for float8_e4m3fn\n            fc2_input_dequant=getattr(\n                module, 'fc2_input_dequant',\n                None),  # activation scale exists only for float8_e4m3fn\n        )\n\n    def load_expert_weights_to_dst(\n            self, module: torch.nn.Module, weights: List[Dict],\n            weight_loading_mode: MoEWeightLoadingMode,\n            load_expert_ids: List[int], dst_w3_w1_weights_tensor: torch.Tensor,\n            dst_w2_weights_tensor: torch.Tensor,\n            dst_w3_w1_bias_tensor: Optional[torch.Tensor],\n            dst_w2_bias_tensor: Optional[torch.Tensor]):\n        # dynamic quant scales for weights\n        self.w3_scales = {}\n        self.w1_scales = {}\n        self.w2_scales = {}\n        # Multithread weight load is superseded by prefetch_files() in model_engine.py\n        # Also, threading adds overhead in order to protect shuffle index cache with critical section.\n        for local_slot_id, expert_id in enumerate(load_expert_ids):\n            # expert_idx is the local slot index of current rank\n            expert_idx = local_slot_id\n\n            if weight_loading_mode == MoEWeightLoadingMode.VANILLA:\n                w1_weight = weights[f\"{expert_id}.w1.weight\"]\n                w3_weight = weights[f\"{expert_id}.w3.weight\"]\n                w2_weight = weights[f\"{expert_id}.w2.weight\"]\n                if module.bias:\n                    w1_bias = weights[f\"{expert_id}.w1.bias\"]\n                    w3_bias = weights[f\"{expert_id}.w3.bias\"]\n                    w2_bias = weights[f\"{expert_id}.w2.bias\"]\n            elif weight_loading_mode == MoEWeightLoadingMode.FUSED_GATE_UP_PROJ:\n                w1_w3_weight = weights[\"gate_up_proj\"][expert_id].transpose(\n                    0, 1)\n                w1_weight, w3_weight = w1_w3_weight.chunk(2, dim=0)\n                w2_weight = weights[\"down_proj\"][expert_id].transpose(\n                    0, 1).contiguous()\n                if module.bias:\n                    w1_w3_bias = weights[\"gate_up_proj.bias\"][expert_id]\n                    w1_bias, w3_bias = w1_w3_bias.chunk(2, dim=0)\n                    w2_bias = weights[\"down_proj.bias\"][expert_id]\n            else:\n                raise NotImplementedError(\n                    f\"Unknown weight loading mode in MoE: {weight_loading_mode}\"\n                )\n\n            w3_scale, w1_scale = self.load_expert_w3_w1_weight(\n                module, w1_weight, w3_weight,\n                dst_w3_w1_weights_tensor[expert_idx])\n\n            w2_scale = self.load_expert_w2_weight(\n                module, w2_weight, dst_w2_weights_tensor[expert_idx])\n            if w3_scale is not None:\n                self.w3_scales[expert_id] = w3_scale\n            if w1_scale is not None:\n                self.w1_scales[expert_id] = w1_scale\n            if w2_scale is not None:\n                self.w2_scales[expert_id] = w2_scale\n\n            if module.bias:\n                self.load_expert_w3_w1_weight(\n                    module,\n                    w1_bias,\n                    w3_bias,\n                    dst_w3_w1_bias_tensor.data[expert_idx],\n dst_w2_bias_tensor.data[expert_idx],\n                                           is_bias=True)\n\n    def _permute_mxfp4_quantize(self, tensor):\n        tensor = tensor.transpose(-2, -1).contiguous()\n        tensor_fp4, tensor_scales = downcast_to_mxfp_torch(tensor,\n                                                           torch.uint8,\n                                                           axis=-2)\n        return tensor_fp4, tensor_scales\n\n    def load_expert_w3_w1_weight(self,\n                                 module: torch.nn.Module,\n                                 w1_weight: torch.Tensor,\n                                 w3_weight: torch.Tensor,\n                                 dst_w3_w1_weight: torch.Tensor,\n                                 is_bias: bool = False):\n        \"\"\"\n        Load w1 and w3 weights for each expert.\n        \"\"\"\n        device = dst_w3_w1_weight.device\n        assert device.type == \"cuda\"\n        # Use full k-padding for float tensors, half for already-packed uint8\n        k_pad = self.k_alignment // 2 if w1_weight.dtype == torch.uint8 else self.k_alignment\n        # n is halved per-branch because we concatenate w1/w3 along N later\n        n_pad = self.n_alignment // 2\n        w1_weight_shard = shard_and_pad_tensor(w1_weight,\n                                               0,\n                                               n_pad,\n                                               k_pad,\n                                               module.tp_size,\n                                               module.tp_rank,\n                                               device=device)\n        w3_weight_shard = shard_and_pad_tensor(w3_weight,\n                                               0,\n                                               n_pad,\n                                               k_pad,\n                                               module.tp_size,\n                                               module.tp_rank,\n                                               device=device)\n\n        if not is_bias and w3_weight_shard.dtype in (torch.bfloat16,\n                                                     torch.float16,\n                                                     torch.float32):\n            # [N, K] -> [K, N]\n            w3_weight_shard, w3_scales = self._permute_mxfp4_quantize(\n                w3_weight_shard)\n            w1_weight_shard, w1_scales = self._permute_mxfp4_quantize(\n                w1_weight_shard)\n            cat_dim = 1\n        else:\n            # [N, K]\n            w3_scales = None\n            w1_scales = None\n            cat_dim = 0\n\n        w31_weight_shard = torch.cat([w3_weight_shard, w1_weight_shard],\n                                     dim=cat_dim)\n\n        # This function is shared by weights and biases, we only do transpose for weights\n        if not is_bias and cat_dim == 0:\n            # Transpose the weights to match the expected format for the Triton gemm kernel\n            w31_weight_shard = w31_weight_shard.transpose(0, 1).contiguous()\n        else:\n            # We use .to here since for Triton the bias is always in float32 and a conversion is needed.\n            w31_weight_shard = w31_weight_shard.to(dst_w3_w1_weight.dtype)\n\n        if self.shuffle_weight:\n            w31_weight_shard = shuffle_weight_for_activation_kernel(\n                w31_weight_shard)\n\n        dst_w3_w1_weight.copy_(w31_weight_shard, non_blocking=True)\n        return (w3_scales, w1_scales)\n\n    def load_expert_w2_weight(self,\n                              module: torch.nn.Module,\n                              w2_weight: torch.Tensor,\n                              dst_w2_weight: torch.Tensor,\n                              is_bias: bool = False):\n        \"\"\"\n        Load w2 weight for each expert.\n        Override this method if you need to preprocess the weights differently.\n        \"\"\"\n        device = dst_w2_weight.device\n        assert device.type == \"cuda\"\n        k_pad = self.k_alignment // 2 if w2_weight.dtype == torch.uint8 else self.k_alignment\n        w2_weight_shard = shard_and_pad_tensor(w2_weight,\n                                               1,\n                                               self.n_alignment,\n                                               k_pad,\n                                               module.tp_size,\n                                               module.tp_rank,\n                                               device=device)\n        w2_scales = None\n\n        if is_bias:\n            # We use .to here since for Triton the bias is always in float32 and a conversion is needed.\n            w2_weight_shard = w2_weight_shard.to(dst_w2_weight.dtype)\n            assert w2_weight_shard.dim() == 1\n            # Handle TP contribution of bias\n            w2_weight_shard /= module.tp_size\n        else:\n            if w2_weight_shard.dtype in (torch.bfloat16, torch.float16,\n                                         torch.float32):\n                # [N, K] -> [K, N]\n                w2_weight_shard, w2_scales = self._permute_mxfp4_quantize(\n                    w2_weight_shard)\n            else:\n                # Transpose the weights to match the expected format for the Triton gemm kernel\n                # [N, K] -> [K, N]\n                w2_weight_shard = w2_weight_shard.transpose(0, 1).contiguous()\n\n        dst_w2_weight.copy_(w2_weight_shard, non_blocking=True)\n\n        return w2_scales\n\n    def _load_expert_w3_w1_weight_scale_mxfp4(\n            self, module: torch.nn.Module, w1_weight_scale: torch.Tensor,\n            w3_weight_scale: torch.Tensor, dst_w3_w1_weight_scale: torch.Tensor,\n            transpose_scales: bool):\n        if transpose_scales:\n            w1_weight_scale = w1_weight_scale.transpose(\n                0, 1)  # (hidden_dim / 32, intermediate_dim)\n            w3_weight_scale = w3_weight_scale.transpose(\n                0, 1)  # (hidden_dim / 32, intermediate_dim)\n\n        # Swapping n_alignment and k_alignment here because we have already transposed\n        w1_weight_scale = shard_and_pad_tensor(\n            w1_weight_scale,\n            1,\n            self.k_alignment // 32,\n            self.n_alignment // 2,\n            module.tp_size,\n            module.tp_rank,\n            device=dst_w3_w1_weight_scale.device)\n\n        w3_weight_scale =            device=dst_w3_w1_weight_scale.device)\n\n        # (hidden_dim / 32, intermediate_dim * 2)\n        combined_scale = torch.cat([w3_weight_scale, w1_weight_scale], dim=1)\n\n        dst_w3_w1_weight_scale.copy_(combined_scale, non_blocking=True)\n\n    def _load_expert_w2_weight_scale_mxfp4(self, module: torch.nn.Module,\n                                           w2_weight_scale: torch.Tensor,\n                                           dst_w2_weight_scale: torch.Tensor,\n                                           transpose_scales: bool):\n        if transpose_scales:\n            w2_weight_scale = w2_weight_scale.transpose(\n                0, 1)  # (intermediate_dim / 32, hidden_dim)\n\n        # k_alignment is divided by 32 because every 32 values share a single scale\n        # Swapping n_alignment and k_alignment here because we have already transposed\n        w2_weight_scale = shard_and_pad_tensor(\n            w2_weight_scale,\n            0,\n            self.k_alignment // 32,\n            self.n_alignment,\n            module.tp_size,\n            module.tp_rank,\n            device=dst_w2_weight_scale.device)\n\n        dst_w2_weight_scale.copy_(w2_weight_scale, non_blocking=True)\n\n    def load_quant_scales(self, module: torch.nn.Module, weights: Dict):\n        # Step1: Load input scales.\n        if self.activation_dtype == torch.float8_e4m3fn:\n            try:\n                max_fc31_input_scale, max_fc2_input_scale = load_activation_scales_fp8_qdq(\n                    module, weights)\n            except KeyError:\n                # We will use dynamic quantization\n                max_fc31_input_scale = None\n                max_fc2_input_scale = None\n\n        # Step2: Load weight scales\n        device = module.w3_w1_weight.device\n        tmp_w3_w1_weight_scale = torch.empty(module.fc31_dequant.shape,\n                                             dtype=torch.uint8,\n                                             device=device)\n        tmp_w2_weight_scale = torch.empty(module.fc2_dequant.shape,\n                                          dtype=torch.uint8,\n                                          device=device)\n        for local_slot_id, expert_id in enumerate(\n                module.initial_local_expert_ids):\n            try:\n                if module.weight_loading_mode == MoEWeightLoadingMode.VANILLA:\n                    w1_weight_scale = weights[f\"{expert_id}.w1.weight_scale\"]\n                    w3_weight_scale = weights[f\"{expert_id}.w3.weight_scale\"]\n                    w2_weight_scale = weights[f\"{expert_id}.w2.weight_scale\"]\n                    need_to_transpose_scales = True\n                elif                       \"gate_up_proj_weight_scale\"][expert_id]\n                    out_dim = combined_weight_scale.shape[-1]\n                    w1_weight_scale = combined_weight_scale[..., :out_dim // 2]\n                    w3_weight_scale = combined_weight_scale[..., out_dim // 2:]\n                    w2_weight_scale = weights[f\"down_proj_weight_scale\"][\n                        expert_id]\n                    need_to_transpose_scales = False\n                else:\n                    raise NotImplementedError(\n                        f\"Unknown weight loading mode in MoE:              w3_weight_scale = self.w3_scales[expert_id]\n                w2_weight_scale = self.w2_scales[expert_id]\n                need_to_transpose_scales = False\n\n            expert_idx = local_slot_id\n\n            self._load_expert_w3_w1_weight_scale_mxfp4(\n                module, w1_weight_scale, w3_weight_scale,\n                tmp_w3_w1_weight_scale[expert_idx], need_to_transpose_scales)\n\n        self.w1_scales.clear()\n        self.w3_scales.clear()\n        self.w2_scales.clear()\n\n        # Scales need to be shuffled as well\n        tmp_w3_w1_weight_scale = shuffle_weight_for_activation_kernel(\n            tmp_w3_w1_weight_scale)\n\n        # Handle w3_w1_weight\n        tmp_w3_w1_weight, tmp_w3_w1_weight_scale =        torch.cuda.empty_cache()\n\n        module.w3_w1_weight = tmp_w3_w1_weight\n        module.fc31_dequant = tmp_w3_w1_weight_scale\n\n        # Handle w2_weight\n        tmp_w2_weight, tmp_w2_weight_scale = swizzle_weight_and_scale(\n            module.w2_weight.data, tmp_w2_weight_scale)\n\n        module._parameters.pop('w2_weight', None)\n        module._parameters.pop('fc2_dequant', None)\n        torch.cuda.empty_cache()\n\n        module.w2_weight = tmp_w2_weight\n        module.fc2_dequant = tmp_w2_weight_scale\n\n        if self.activation_dtype == torch.float8_e4m3fn:\n            if max_fc31_input_scale is None or max_fc2_input_scale is None:\n                module.fc31_input_dequant = None\n                module.fc2_input_dequant = None\n            else:\n                module.fc31_input_dequant.data.copy_(max_fc31_input_scale,\n                                                     non_blocking=True)\n                module.fc2_input_dequant.data.copy_(max_fc2_input_scale,\n                                                    non_blocking=True)\n\n    def apply(self, module: torch.nn.Module, x: torch.Tensor,\n              router_logits: torch.Tensor) -> torch.Tensor:\n        # Fetch all the data needed for the Triton kernel\n        if self.activation_dtype == torch.float8_e4m3fn:\n            if module.fc31_input_dequant is None:\n                hidden_states, hidden_states_scale = torch.ops.tensorrt_llm.quantize_e4m3_per_tensor(\n                    x)\n            else:\n                hidden_states, _ = torch.ops.tensorrt_llm.static_quantize_e4m3_per_tensor(\n                    x, module.fc31_input_dequant)\n                hidden_states_scale = module.fc31_input_dequant\n        else:\n            hidden_states = x\n        expert_logits = router_logits\n        gemm1_weights = module.w3_w1_weight\n        gemm1_scales = module.fc31_dequant\n        gemm2_weights = module.w2_weight\n        gemm2_scales = module.fc2_dequant\n        top_k = module.routing_method.experts_per_token\n\n        # hidden_states: (num_tokens, hidden_dim) torch.float8_e4m3fn\n        # hidden_states_scale: (,) torch.float32\n        # expert_logits: (num_tokens, num_experts) torch.bfloat16\n        # gemm1_weights: (num_experts, hidden_dim / 2, intermediate_dim * 2) torch.uint8\n        # gemm1_scales: (num_experts, hidden_dim / 32, intermediate_dim * 2) torch.uint8\n        # gemm2_weights: (num_experts, intermediate_dim / 2, hidden_dim) torch.uint8\n        # gemm2_scales: (num_experts, intermediate_dim / 32, hidden_dim) torch.float32\n\n        # Step 1: Routing\n        num_experts = expert_logits.shape[1]\n        if num_experts > 1:\n            rdata, gather_indx, scatter_indx = TritonEPRouter()(\n                expert_logits,\n                top_k,\n                ep=module.ep_size,\n                node_idx=module.ep_rank)\n        else:\n            rdata, gather_indx, scatter_indx = None, None, None\n\n        # Step 2: Gemm1\n        # Setup quantization context\n        def _maybe_pad_activation(hidden_states):\n            k_dim = hidden_states.shape[-1]\n            padded_k_dim = get_padded_size(k_dim, self.k_alignment)\n            hidden_states = torch.nn.functional.pad(hidden_states,\n                                                    (0, padded_k_dim - k_dim))\n            return hidden_states\n\n        if self.activation_dtype ==
